name:Gâ€uâ€eâ€sâ€tâ€ â€Uâ€sâ€eâ€r
info:Hotel Deluxe Hot Spring Suite (2 beds)
info:Stayed in May 2024
info:Friends
info:38 Reviews
rating:4.7
posted:Posted May 4, 2024
msg:This is my first time here after the epidemic. I liked Yihe before. It is indeed a little worse than before, but I also found that some rooms in the hotel have been renovated. Although the room type I stayed in this time is still the carpeted one, the maintenance is relatively good. There is a little smell, which is acceptable. Just ventilate and turn on the air conditioner. It may be affected by the weather. But I really recommend that the hotel only have carpets in the bed area, and change other areas to wooden boards or floor tiles. This is more suitable for suites with hot springs. Other toiletries are still good. I like that the hot spring water is hot and slippery. It is a real hot spring and can be used unlimited times. We opened the water in advance and went to have breakfast. There is no need to add too much cold water to ensure that it is all hot spring water.
The service is also good, and the breakfast variety is OK. The environment is beautiful, the public area is hygienic, the pool is large and many, there are hot mineral deposits, and sauna steaming. Itâ€™s just that towels are limited, unlike before when they were available everywhere. The nearby Chaihuo Huangshen Restaurant is not far away. Some newly built homestays in the back mountain can be visited. Overall, I am not disappointed. It is not as bad as some online reviews describe. I guess the hotel has made some improvements. I will choose to come again in the future

msg:It's about half an hour's drive from Taishan city center via online taxi. There is a private pool on the room terrace for you to soak in, and there is a special public pool downstairs. Breakfast and afternoon tea are also included.
The carpet in the room is very dusty and the facilities are a bit old. The scenery in the odd-numbered rooms is mediocre, while the even-numbered rooms have a wide view.
The breakfast selection is rich and delicious, but the lunch selection is a bit mediocre with only packaged meals. In the evening, I went to the Chinese restaurant in the hotel to eat. The price was not expensive and the taste was good. The barbecue snack on the road from the hotel to the public pond was also very delicious and the taste was in line with my taste. There are many restaurants near the hotel to try
